4.4 Customer Service Quality and Satisfaction
Yang Ming adheres to the service philosophies and policies of Teamwork, Innovation, Integrity, and 
Pragmatism and is devoted to offering customers high-quality services. For operational strategies, we 
enhance the efficiency of integrating global operational resources by collaborating with other well-
known carriers around the world. As for customer management, the Company has developed customer 
relationship management policies and kept in close touch with local agents and sales employees on a daily 
basis to understand customers’ needs and market trends and thereby make timely responses.
In order to enhance customer satisfaction and service quality, the Company has organized the “From 
Responsibility to Accountability” course that helps build employees’ awareness of service quality and 
personal accountability and motivates them to comply with the three main principles for handling 
customer complaints: listening, apologizing, and being lenient, put themselves in customers’ shoes, show 
empathy, understand the customers’ needs, and provide assistance with a positive and active attitude. 
In the event of circumstances where customers incur damage, ﬁrst-line sales personnel and local agents 
should understand and listen to the customers’ problems, discuss with the relevant personnel from 
the headquarters and develop solutions, and then notify the Cargo Loss Claim Team of the Insurance & 
Claim Department. Relevant departments should ﬁnd out the roots of the problems and who should be 
accountable for them. The Sales Department serves as the coordinator responsible for giving instructions 
to local agents and handling the problems in comprehensive ways acceptable to the customers, thereby 
maintaining good customer relationships and promoting future relationship development.
■ Customer Complaint Handling Process
■ Customer Satisfaction Survey
Oriented towards customer needs, Yang Ming continues to deepen the logistics services, enhance 
service quality, create values for customers, and optimize procedures through digital transformation to 
respond to the customers’ requirements in a timely manner.
We conduct a customer satisfaction survey every 2 years, where customer samples are provided by 
the Sales Department and agents worldwide. In the survey performed in 2022, 1,634 questionnaires 
were distributed, of which 1,078 were returned, with a return rate of 65.97%. The questionnaires 
covered 7 service aspects: booking and delivery, containers, quotation and rating, documentation 
quality, customer services, e-commerce, and customer complaints and provided open-ended 
questions for customers to answer. For any unsatisfactory feedback from customers, we ask the 
agents to contact the customers, provide solutions and require the agents to ask the customers 
if they are satisﬁed with subsequent improvements and report the results to the E-commerce & 
Documentation Department. The E-commerce & Documentation Department organizes complaint 
records for the headquarters’ Sales Department’s reference at the end of each quarter and 
follows up on the customers to see if they become satisﬁed and continue to do business with the 
Company.

5.1 Human Rights Policy and Diverse  
       Communication Channels
5.1.1 Yang Ming’s Human Rights Policy
■ Human Rights Policy and Declaration
Yang Ming has operated worldwide for a long time and has been dedicated to respecting and maintaining 
internationally acknowledged human rights and ensuring the compliance of business activities with 
local laws and regulations as well as international standards, thereby providing a fair and equal working 
environment and making sure that the rights and interests of our employees and partners are respected 
and protected. When it comes to human rights, we respect and protect all internationally acknowledged 
human rights and never engage in any activities that neglect and involve human rights violations. The 
Company’s Human Rights Policy has been developed based on the International Bill of Human Rights, 
the United National Global Compact, and the human rights conventions of the International Labour 
Organization. Internal rules and regulations have been established. For violations of laws and regulations 
or the Company’s internal regulations, punishments are given according to relevant punishment policies.
Yang Ming has committed to upholding internationally 
proclaimed human rights in the locations where we 
operate without any unfair treatment arising from 
ethnicity or gender, ensuring the freedom of association 
and collective bargaining rights, respecting privacy, caring 
for the underprivileged, forbidding the use of child labor, 
prohibiting harassment, and banning forced labor. We 
have also strived to eliminate all forms of forced labor 
and discrimination in recruitment and employment. 
The Company offers reasonable working conditions, 
maintains the physical and mental health of employees, 
endeavors to reduce factors hazardous to safety and 
health, and ensures thorough protection of the personal 
privacy of all customers, employees and stakeholders, 
fulﬁlling human rights protection responsibilities. 
 
■ Human Rights Education and Training
The Company’s education, training, and propaganda on the Human Rights Policy aim at raising 
employees’ awareness of human rights protection. The Company organized a 0.5-hour course for all 
onshore employees in 2022, and 1,428 employees completed the course, with a test pass rate of up to 
92.5%.
■ Human Rights Due Diligence
International organizations have established relevant conventions and standards for the shipping industry 
and emphasized that vessel operators must further develop their human rights regulations. To raise 
awareness of seafarers’ rights, the seafarers have asked their companies to provide corresponding 
protection measures. The Company takes human rights issues seriously and introduced the concept of 
human rights due diligence in March 2023. By analyzing the trends of international human rights issues, 
interviewing internal oﬃcers, and reviewing internal labor-management documents, the human rights 
issues are summarized and presented to the head of each department and oﬃce for assessment. These 
questionnaires cover Yang Ming’s own operations for assessment and contain 25 issues categorized 
into 4 groups, namely labor rights, health and safety, environment and community, and governance 
and morality. We hope to identify our own operational risks through these assessment questionnaires. 
The initial assessment results indicate that none of the issues are considered high-risk issues. 18 issues 
are medium-risk issues and the other 7 are low-risk issues. In the future, the Company will use the initial 
assessment results as the basis to initiate an oﬃcial human rights due diligence process with the aim of 
progressively deepening and expanding human rights as well as planning and executing relevant risk 
mitigation and subsequent remedial measures based on the identiﬁed potential risks.
● Human Rights Risk Issue Identification Process
Human Rights Policy 
of YangMing Marine 
Transport Corp.
International Human Rights Standards
Identify human rights issues in the shipping industry according to the International Bill of 
Human Rights, UN Global Compact, the human rights conventions of the International Labour 
Organization, and the Geneva Declaration on Human Rights at Sea.
01
Internal Data Review
Pore over labor-management meeting records, employee feedback, records of special events, 
and MSCI ratings to determine potential human rights risks.
02
Interviews with the Management
Have interviews with Yang Ming’s top level and middle level management to understand if the 
Company has had any event involving human rights infringement recently to determine events 
with human rights risks.
03
Questionnaire Preparation/Distribution
Prepare questionnaires according to the International Bill of Human Rights, internal data 
review results, and the interviews with the top-level management, discuss with Yang Ming’s 
team, and have Yang Ming’s middle-level management complete the questionnaires.
04
Questionnaire Result Assessment
Analyze the answers in the questionnaires to identify the human rights risk issues that Yang 
Ming should take seriously.

5.1.2 Smooth Communication Channels
■ Complaint Channels for Onshore Employees
Yang Ming’s Human Resources Department is responsible for managing the employee 
mailbox and complaint hotline that allow employees to express their opinions in a real-
time manner simply via email. When encountering discrimination, sexual harassment, 
and workplace violence in the workplace, the employees can file a complaint through the 
Chairman’s mailbox, independent directors’ mailbox, or independent reporting mailbox 
(managed by the Chief Audit Executive and designated person) or to the department 
concerned. Any person can report any illegal act or violation of the work rules, Codes of 
Ethical Conduct, Ethical Corporate Management Best Practice Principles, and Procedures for 
Ethical Management and Guidelines for Conduct through the aforesaid channels.
■ Complaint Channels for Seafarers
To understand the thoughts of seafarers, the Company carries out 4 questionnaire surveys 
during seafarer training, including a survey on complaint channels for the seafarers 
and has an independent complaint mailbox and a sexual harassment whistleblowing 
mailbox in place for the seafarers, which can only be accessed by the Chief Marine 
Technology Officer and the Head of the Maritime Department. A sexual harassment 
whistleblowing hotline was also provided for the seafarers to submit suggestions and 
complaints. In addition, all the Company’s vessels have acquired a “Maritime Labour 
Convention”
Note certiﬁcate and complied with the requirements of international conventions. 
Note: The “Maritime Labour Convention” (MLC) is a labor protection standard convention established by the International Labour Organization and 
          aims to ensure that the working and living rights of all seafarers are protected and promote the sustainable development of international trade 
           and shipping.
■ Labor-management Meetings
To ensure smooth labor-management communication, the Company organizes at least one 
labor-management meeting per quarter. In 2022, 4 labor-management meetings were held.
■ Freedom of Association
In support of the UN Global Compact, the Company ensures that all employees have the 
freedom of association, and all seafarers can choose by themselves if they join any union 
of seafarers. The Company has also set up a marine union for over 22 years, and the 
employees may join or withdraw as they wish. The Company currently has harmonious labor-
management relations and does not enter into any collective bargaining agreement.
For the prevention of sexual harassment and illegal violence, please refer to 5.4.2 Health 
Management and Care - Prevention of Illegal Infringement
After receiving complaints and suggestions from onshore employees and seafarers, the 
Company replies to the employees one by one and handles the complaints and suggestions 
properly and reasonably. For their detailed numbers and types, please refer to the following:

5.2 Talent Recruitment and Cultivation
5.2.1 Talent Recruitment
■ Talent Management Policy
Yang Ming endeavors to create an open-minded, inclusive, diverse and respectful working 
environment and develops talent recruitment strategies based on the Company’s short-term/
medium-term/long-term plans to attract the most excellent talent to join the team. The safety 
and operating eﬃciency of the ﬂeet correlate closely to the abilities of seafarers, who are the 
most important factor to the operation of the ﬂeet. The Company continuously recruits talent 
aspiring to work as seafarers and provides good career development opportunities to ensure 
that the team has the most excellent talent, thereby enhancing the operation of the ﬂeet.

■ Seafarer Safety Management
To improve sailing safety, the Company has developed relevant safety management policies 
and measures according to the ISM CODE in response to the risks of changing weather and 
medical inconveniences that seafarers face when working on ships and set up the Fleet 
Quality Management Team and Fleet Management Team A. Through the shipboard audit and 
supervision or the boarding visit mechanism, the overall ship operation and sailing safety 
were elevated. The training for seafarers aims to improve their competences and raising their 
occupational health and safety awareness by elaborating on the maritime cases, the ISM 
policy of the Company, and the latest conventions, laws and regulations. In light of the call for 
emissions reduction to protect the environment in recent years, the seafarer training was also 
improved to include courses on clean energy for ships and compliance with environmental 
regulations worldwide.
■ Employee Development
Based on the all-around talent cultivation policy, the Company encourages employees to gain 
experience from working in a diﬀerent unit or even overseas after staying in the same position for 2 
or 3 years to build enough competency in order to develop comprehensive skills. The Company will 
continue to promote employee rotation which is the key to the Company’s talent development.
■ Training Hours
In the future, we will continue implementing overseas apprenticeship plans and other 
relevant programs to dispatch employees with potential to each regional center overseas for 
training or apprenticeship to broaden their global horizons.

Appendix
Deepening Shipping Talent Cultivation
Yang Ming has been devoted to promoting the culture and education 
in the shipping industry and has not fallen behind in developing young 
students. We hope to have talent better equipped with professional 
shipping knowledge and skills through the delivery of diverse education, 
thereby achieving the long-term development and prosperity of the 
Company. As such, the Company has actively implemented various 
industry-academia collaboration and education/training programs to 
make maritime education better ﬁt the industry and deepen hands-on 
teaching to inspire and facilitate the growth and development of young 
people.
The Company widely recruits talents and actively increases industry-
academia exchange and collaboration opportunities to develop 
talent interested in the shipping industry and aspiring to work in the 
industry. In 2022, 16 interns were enrolled in 6 programs in the hope of 
equipping young students with industrial knowledge and skills in a face-
to-face manner and fostering overall competitiveness.
■ Yang Ming’s Letters of Intent with Educational Institutions and Organizations
●Cooperation agreement signed with National Taiwan Ocean 
      University
● Letter of intent signed with National Kaohsiung University of 
      Science and Technology
●Cooperation agreement on seafarer talent cultivation signed 
      with Taipei University of Marine Technology
●Letter of intent for industry-academia collaboration with 
      National Penghu Marine & Fishery Vocational High School
●Memorandum of understanding with the Affiliated Keelung 
    Maritime Senior High School of National Taiwan Ocean 
      University
● Cooperation agreement with National Suao Marine & Fisheries Vocational High School
● Mariner Training Program of the Maritime and Port Bureau, Ministry of Transportation and Communications
● Memorandum of understanding for the promotion of industrial training for veterans
■ Post-baccalaureate Programs and Courses to  
    Nurture New Generations
The Company teamed up with National Taiwan Ocean University 
and the Department of Shipping Technology of National Kaohsiung 
University of Science and Technology (NKUST) to continue launching 
post-baccalaureate merchant marine and marine engineering courses 
and programs. In the post-baccalaureate diverse expertise development 
courses and programs, professors from National Taiwan Ocean 
University are responsible for delivering professional shipping-speciﬁc 
knowledge and skills. In addition to basic shipping practices, the courses 
and programs even cover international conventions and maritime 
regulations, navigation English, navigation, and many other contents. 
Moreover, the students are provided with hands-on courses on engine 
room and bridge resource management, radar operation, etc. as well 
as lessons given by instructors from the industry, helping them get the 
big picture of marine transportation. Yang Ming also provides marine 
internship and service opportunities enabling students to apply what 
they have learned.
Marine Talent Cultivation Outcomes in 2022
●Officers: 47 students enrolled in the post-baccalaureate merchant marine and marine 
   engineering program continuously launched by Yang Ming together with National Taiwan 
   Ocean University in Keelung ; 18 students enrolled in the post-baccalaureate shipping 
    technology program jointly launched by Yang Ming and the NKUST.
●Ratings: 29 students enrolled in the rating training program launched by Yang Ming and 
   the NKUST in Kaohsiung ; 31 students participated in the rating training program jointly 
    organized by Yang Ming and the Chinese Maritime Institute (as well as the Veterans Aﬀairs 
   Council) in Wanli ; 9 students enrolled in the rating training program launched by Yang 
    Ming together with the NTUT.
●Students are provided with maritime internship opportunities. There were 38 sailing and 
     marine engineering interns from the three maritime universities.

■ Upgrading Industry-Academia Equipment
In 2022, the Chairman signed memorandums of understanding (MOU) for industry-
academia collaboration with National Taiwan Ocean University, National Kaohsiung 
University of Science and Technology, the Aﬃliated Keelung Maritime Senior High 
School of National Taiwan Ocean University, and National Suao Marine & Fisheries 
Vocational High School, donated the latest ship maneuvering simulation equipment 
to National Kaohsiung University of Science and Technology, upgraded the Multi-
Function Ship Handling Simulator system of National Taiwan Ocean University and 
donated a global maritime distress safety system (GMDSS) simulator to it. This can 
not only facilitate the provision of formal education and training in the future, but 
also equip students with more abilities and skills that prepare them to engage in the 
industry and workforce immediately after graduation. Also, maritime and seafarers 
can have better access to on-the-job training and research, boosting navigation and 
transportation safety and the cultivation of shipping talent.
■ Project Research
Project
Research Description
Project 1: Research on Merchant 
Ships’ Use of Methanol Fuel
Analyze and assess the feasibility of using methanol as 
alternative energy for container ships in the future in the 
hope that the use of methanol can be taken into account for 
the selection of equipment for newly built vessels.
Project 2: Research and Discussion 
on the Ballast Water Treatment 
Methods Applicable to Container 
Ships
Analyze the cost-effectiveness and biological treatment 
eﬀect of chemical agents in treating vessel ballast water.

5.3 Employee Compensation and Beneﬁts
■ Employee Compensation and Benefits
Yang Ming strives to offer highly competitive compensation and benefits to attract and 
retain excellent employees. The Company’s overall compensation policy adheres to the 
philosophy of equal pay for equal work. There is no gender gap in the starting salary of entry-
level employees. The basic starting salary of new hires was increased from NT$36,000 to 
NT$43,600 in 2022, growing by 21.1%. In comparison to the basic starting salary in Taiwan 
in 2022, which was NT$25,250, the starting salary offered by the Company was extremely 
competitive in the job market. The salary of non-managerial full-time employees is published 
on the Market Observation Post System on time as required.

Life Insurance 
(Group Insurance)
The main purpose of “general employee group insurance” taken out in 2022 is to provide life and ﬁnancial 
protection for employees and their families when the employees themselves and their dependents 
need hospitalization due to injury or illness or, unfortunately, pass away or become disabled during the 
employees’ service in the Company. Initially, 1,520 people were insured, with NT$5,320,244 spent. The 
number of insureds may increase or decrease every month based on the number of employees.
Trust
● Employee Stock Ownership Trust:Yang Ming offers a 30% subsidy to encourage all employees to 
     participate in the stock ownership trust plan and purchase the Company’s shares.
● Employee Savings Trust:We provide a 20% subsidy to encourage employees to build wealth over 
     the long term by participating in the beneﬁt fund trust plan.
Health Check-ups
● Better frequencies than those required by law are provided, namely once per year for personnel over 
     40 years old and once per 2 years for those below 40 years old.
● The health check-up allowance was increased to NT$10,000.
● One-day oﬃcial leave is granted.
Appropriation of 
Beneﬁt Funds
The Company appropriates 1.5‰ of operating income and deducts and uses 5‰ of employees’ salary monthly as 
beneﬁt funds in order for the Employee Welfare Committee to provide various beneﬁts.
Paid Personal 
/Sick Leave
In addition to the leave as required by the provisions of the Labor Standards Act, onshore employees are provided 
with 5 days of paid personal/sick leave each year, so that they can have ﬂexibility when they have to go on leave. 
Due to the nature of the work of seafarers, relevant shore leave is provided in accordance with the provisions of 
the Seafarer Act.
Flextime System
The system enables employees to adjust their working hours ﬂexibly to not only avoid the trouble of commuting 
during rush hours, but also make it convenient to take care of their families or pick up their children.
Retirement 
Pension
Yang Ming’s employee retirement policy has been established based on the “Labor Standards Act” and “Labor 
Pension Act.” The Company makes a monthly pension contribution to designated accounts to ensure the 
contribution and payment of employees’ pensions, thereby further encouraging their long-term service in the 
Company and growth with us.
Subsidies and 
Allowances
Allowances in 2022 – Number of employees receiving/beneﬁted amount invested/of the allowances
● Birthday cash gift – 2,057 recipients; NTD 10,285 (thousand)
● Wedding cash gift – 41 recipients; NTD 205 (thousand)
● Retirement cash gift – 37 recipients; NTD 370 (thousand)
● Hospitalization beneﬁt – 68 recipients; NTD 136 (thousand)
● Childbirth allowance – 24 recipients; NTD 120 (thousand)
● Education allowance for employees’ children (2 times per year) – 1,094 recipients; NTD 4,763 (thousand) 
● Scholarship for employees’ children (2 times per year) – 162 recipients; NTD 810 (thousand)
Wedding Gold 
Accessories
 In order to enhance the happiness of employees' families, Yang Ming holds an annual commemoration for the 40th, 
30th, 20th and 10th anniversary of their marriages, where each family is given 22.5 grams, 18.75 grams, 15 grams, or 
11.25 grams of gold accessories, respectively. In 2022, a total of 63 employees received the gold accessories.
Preschool Center
To support the public childcare policy implemented by the government and provide a more convenient and friendly 
working environment for childcare for employees, the Company set up a cooperative preschool service center at the 
Xin Yi oﬃce building in Keelung, which was oﬃcially put into service on August 15, 2022. The preschool center enrolls 
preschoolers at the age of 2-6 and prioritizes the children and grandchildren of the employees. The monthly tuition 
is only NT$2,000, which is the same as that of non-proﬁt kindergartens, signiﬁcantly reducing the parenting and 
ﬁnancial burden of the employees. With the center, the employees are able to give birth to and raise children with 
no worries and ensure work-family balance, facilitating a childcare-friendly workplace.
Club Activities
There were 26 clubs in 2022, including table tennis, badminton, golf, volleyball, tennis, basketball, 
swimming, bowling, aerobic dance, and yoga clubs.

5.4 Occupational Safety 
and Health
5.4.1 Occupational Safety and Health 
           Promotion and Maintenance
■ Yang Ming’s Occupational Safety and  
     Health Management Policy
The Company offers international marine transportation 
services and values personnel safety, vessel safety, 
and cargo safety during transportation. To implement 
the occupational safety and health policy of “ensuring 
occupational safety and promoting the physical and 
mental health of employees,” Yang Ming was certiﬁed to 
ISO 45001 Occupational Health and Safety Management 
Systems in 2019 and became the ﬁrst ISO45001-certiﬁed 
carrier in Taiwan. We were also certified by Taiwan 
Occupational Safety and Health Management Systems 
(TOSHMS). Relevant certiﬁcates have been disclosed on the 
Company’s oﬃcial website. The Company’s occupational 
safety and health management system covers 100% of the 
Company’s operations, including relevant vessel container 
transportation management, customer service, terminal 
container loading/unloading, cargo storage, and freight 
forwarding practices, as well as employees (99%) and non-
employees (1%) in the Company’s premises in Taiwan.
The Company set up the “Occupational Safety and Health Committee” in accordance with the Regulations of Occupational Safety and Health Management. 
The committee consists of 9 members who are occupational safety and health personnel, relevant department heads, and labor representatives, of which 
3 are labor representatives. All safety and health performance indicators for occupational safety and health education and training, health management, 
and occupational disease prevention are reviewed at Occupational Safety and Health Committee meetings every quarter. In addition to giving advice on 
improvements and response measures, the occupational safety and health proposals presented by all departments and workers are discussed, and the 
results are communicated throughout the Company to improve workplace and environmental safety for the employees and facilitate healthcare.

■ Work-Related Injury Statistics
The Company has spared no eﬀort to implement ﬁeld safety and health management and enhance 
prevention practices. Since the Keelung (Yang Ming) Container Yard started to report its accident-free 
work hours in 2006, there have been any work-related accidents for 16 consecutive years. As of the end 
of December 2022, the Keelung (Yang Ming) Container Yard ’s accident-free work hours have reached 
1,282,352 hours (1.282 million hours), and the number has been continuously increasing.
■ Contractors’ Occupational Safety and Health Management
The Company sees contractors as important partners. To ensure the safety of their employees 
at work, in addition to holding coordination organization meetings, ensuring prior notiﬁcation 
of hazards, and supervising operations in compliance with the laws and regulations related to 
occupational safety and health, all workplaces promote various management mechanisms to 
strengthen the contractors’ safety and health management. A contractor qualiﬁcation review 
procedure has been established, where contractors are required to complete a sustainability 
statement and a qualiﬁcation review form, as well as to abide by the laws and regulations on 
labor health and safety in working environments, strive to provide employees with a safe and 
health working environment, and organize comprehensive occupational safety and health 
education and training for them in order to reduce the probability of occurrence of accidents 
or incidents and protect the employees’ legal rights. After being evaluated by relevant units, 
qualified contractors are classified, and a “List of Qualified Contractors” is created. The 
qualiﬁed contractors in the list will be ﬁrst invited by procurement departments to bid. This 
procedure will help procurement departments better understand contractors while improving 
the construction quality and safety level of contracted works in practical aspects. The Company 
attended 24 coordination organization meetings in 2022.
There were no employees suffering occupational diseases 
and serious work-related accidents in the Company in 2022
■ Information on Work-Related Accidents
According to the Group’s annual risk assessment report and result in 2022, containing information 
summarized from the risk assessment forms returned by all units, multiple units mentioned personnel 
safety risk when it came to operational risks. It was found that a majority of accidents were traffic 
accidents during commuting. However, there were some accidents involving operational errors that 
led to personnel injuries and fatalities, and most of them occurred during ﬁeld operations (in container 
terminals/on vessels). Relevant units have come up with corresponding control measures to reduce the 
frequency of risk occurrence. For example, in September 2022, an injury accident occurred on one of 
the Company’s R.O.C. vessels as a result of a lifting operation. The injured seafarer has recovered and 
returned to work in the ﬂeet. The Company has asked the entire ﬂeet to further emphasize the safety 
of lifting operations. The Company’s employee disabling injury frequency rate, disabling injury severity 
rate, number of employees suﬀering serious work-related accidents, and other work-related accident 
indicators between 2020 and 2022 were lower than the industry’s averages.

■ Risk Assessment in Workplaces
The Company has established the “Safety and Health Risk and Opportunity Management 
Procedures” to carry out risk assessment in the workplace.In 2022, the Company’s workplaces in 
Taiwan identiﬁed 147 operational items, and a total of 560 operational risks and 44 operational 
opportunities were assessed and reviewed throughout the Company’s workplaces. The level of the 
risks was determined based on the risk matrix and risk rating table. There were about 3% of the 
items that were high-risk items in the operations, and improvement measures such as engineering 
control, management control, and personal protective equipment were adopted according to 
assessment results to reduce the level of risk to which the items were exposed from high to low. 
The assessment results were then submitted to the Occupational Safety and Health Committee for 
review and approval. The contents of risk and opportunity assessment forms are reviewed every 
year and used as principles for safety and health management strategies. In addition, working 
environment monitoring, continuous management, and tracking/assessment are also conducted.
Yang Ming is well aware that employees are an important asset for the Company and therefore 
endeavors to provide employees onboard and onshore with safe and healthy working environments 
based on risk and opportunity assessment results, comply with occupational safety laws and regulations, 
and formulate related operational procedures to ensure the safety and health of the employees.
■ Occupational Safety and Health Education and Training
Yang Ming has an occupational safety and health management plan as well as safety and health work 
rules in place to perform periodic inspections, prioritized inspections, operating inspections, and on-site 
inspections and implement employee safety and health education and training in order to ensure that 
every worker is familiar with the laws and regulations related to occupational safety and health, safety 
and health work rules, and related knowledge and skills. In 2022, 36 education and training sessions on 
the safety of onshore employees were organized, with 467 trainees in total.
To protect the safety and health of workers eﬀectively, the Company arranges training based on their 
types of work, operating environments, and other important factors and according to the probability 
of risk occurrence and the level of impact on the Company’s operations, including periodic retraining 
for the Chief Occupational Safety and Health Oﬃcer, occupational safety and health managers, and 
Occupational Safety Committee members, regular retraining for labor health service nurses, and 
training for new employees and existing employees. A total of 3 training sessions have been organized.
■ Safety Culture Enhancement
In an eﬀort to enhance employees’ safety awareness, the idea of prevention is incorporated into 
their daily work routine to ensure the sustainable development of the Company and achieve 
personnel safety, vessel safety and cargo safety. The following are our continuous efforts to 
promote a safety culture:
1.Valuing vessels’ safety culture: In 2022, to improve vessel operation safety and eﬀectively 
identify dangerous areas onboard, there were 360 oﬃcers and 4 superintendents completing 
the Class 3 occupational safety and health manager training as of December 31, 2022, which 
was above and beyond what the laws require.
2.Continuously performing onboard emergency response exercises 
Please refer to “5.2.2 Talent Cultivation-Seafarer Safety Management” for details.
3.Enhancing dangerous good management in harbor areas: Even though a dangerous 
good storage area has been set up in Yang Ming’s container yard in Keelung, to enhance 
dangerous good management in operational sites and facilitate disaster prevention and 
emergency response, the Company has conducted education and communication on disaster 
prevention, thereby improving the professional competency of employees handling dangerous 
goods, consolidating dangerous good safety and management culture, and ensuring a 
sound prevention and response organization, manpower and equipment. This can allow for 
proper disaster control and recovery in a short period of time in order to ensure the safety of 
personnel, environment and property and minimize impacts. The “Dangerous Good Storage 
Management Plan” established in accordance with the “Regulations on Port Services at 
Commercial Ports” was implemented after being submitted to and approved by the Port of 
Keelung, Taiwan International Ports Corporation. 4 Class A dangerous goods officers and 1 
Class B dangerous goods oﬃcer were also designated, more than the number required by law. 
The aforesaid oﬃcers should have a certiﬁcate of completion after being trained and qualiﬁed 
by the Maritime Port Bureau, and receive periodic retraining.
● Workplace Inspection Actions
Item
Description
Drinking water 
equipment
According to the Environmental Protection Administration’s “Regulations Governing the 
Use and Maintenance of Stationary Equipment for Continuous Supply of Drinking Water,” 
stationary equipment installed in public or private premises for continuous supply of drinking 
water for the public shall be maintained or inspected by the individuals/organizations in 
charge of the equipment or professional vendors. The Company conducts water quality 
inspections in accordance with the provision.
The water source of the building is tap water, and the water dispensers installed are sampled 
and tested for water quality and Escherichia coli by a testing body accredited by the central 
competent authority every 3 months. A “water quality inspection record” is prepared 
according to the result and clearly pasted on each dispenser.
Air conditioning 
equipment
The equipment is governed by the “Procedures for the Management and Maintenance of 
Electromechanical Equipment in Yang Ming’s Cidu Building.”
The mesh ﬁlters of the air handling unit on each ﬂoor are cleaned once a month, and the 
cleaning works are recorded in the “Air Conditioning Mesh Filter Maintenance Record.”
Maintenance of water chiller units: The water chiller units are maintained and serviced by 
external vendors once a quarter. In the ﬁrst quarter of every year, the drain clearing process 
is conducted, and the units undergo full maintenance at least every 3 years.
Air Quality
The Company performs CO2 monitoring every 6 months as required by law, and all 
values observed have been below the statutory threshold, ensuring a comfortable office 
environment for employees.
Food safety
The Company has set up the Mess Committee, undergone irregular sampling inspections by 
external hygiene bodies, and obtained a hygiene management rating mark in recognition of 
our performance.

5.4.2 Health Management and Care
● Comprehensive Health Care
■ Increase of Health Checkup Frequencies and Allowance 
In 2022, the Company conducted a regular health checkup for employees, where the health 
checkup allowance was increased to NT$10,000, and there were 637 employees eligible for 
the allowance. Yang Ming also went above and beyond what the law requires by adjusting the 
health checkup frequencies as follows: “once per year for employees over 40 years of age; 
once per 2 years for those below 40 years of age” and granted an oﬃcial leave, providing 
all employees with better health care. In addition, the health checkup was deliberately 
designed based on the incidence rate of the top 10 most common cancers in Taiwan, 
enabling the employees to choose the health checkup package that best suits them based on 
their individual health conditions, age and family health history. The employees rated their 
satisfaction with the health checkup in 2022 at nearly 5 points, almost hitting the perfect 
score.  
After this health checkup, the employees’ health risks were classiﬁed based on the level of 
abnormality and abnormal items in the results and tracked subsequently. As most employees 
participating in this health checkup were middle aged, the statistical analysis found that a 
higher proportion of employees were at medium or high risk of “developing cardiovascular 
diseases in 10 years.” The analysis also indicated that a majority of employees were 
overweight, and this might be correlated to the global widespread of COVID-19, a substantial 
reduction in exercise volume, and a more unbalanced diet. Therefore, after the annual health 
checkup was completed, we organized the “Walk Towards Health 2022” campaign. 462 
employees signed up for the campaign, of which 276 won the “Goal Achieved Award.”
■ Construction of Emergency Medical Aid Mechanisms 
We installed automated external deﬁbrillators (AEDs) in our 6 premises in Taiwan, and inspect 
and check them regularly. Moreover, our ﬁrst aider deployment is better than that required 
by law. As of the end of 2022, there were 51 employees who are qualified first aiders in 
Taiwan, and personnel retraining has been organized periodically.
■ Employment of Doctors and Nurses for Health Management and Health 
     Promotion Activities 
The Company employed 3 on-site health service doctors and 3 professional nurses as 
required by law to provide employees with professional health management and consultation 
services in corporate health management and promotion activities. 
Operations in harbor areas are of high risk. To maintain operational safety in the Keelung (Yang 
Ming) Container Yard and enhance employees’ dangerous goods awareness and emergency 
response, the container terminal organizes regular dangerous goods training annually as well 
as one fire extinguishing, reporting and evacuation drill at least every 6 months to reduce 
the probability of fire occurrence, and unfortunately, in case of any emergency, utilize fire 
extinguishing equipment while eﬀectively deploying proper manpower to quickly handle the 
emergency, put out the ﬁre promptly, and minimize the damage.
Yang Ming’s Workplace Occupational Safety Education/Training and Outcomes: 
● 1 dangerous goods training session, with 23 trainees and at least 2 training hours 
    per trainee.
● Designated 4 Class A dangerous goods oﬃcer and 1 Class B dangerous goods oﬃcer.
● 374employees participated in workplace ﬁre drills.
● 360 oﬃcers and 4 ship superintendents completed the Class 3 occupational safety 
    and health manager training.
● 36 education and training sessions on the safety of onshore employees, 
    with 467 trainees.

■ Health Lectures 
The Company has organized health lectures to increase employees’ knowledge of health and 
encourage them to build good habits in life. In 2022, 25 health lectures were held, with 2,818 
participants. These lectures could help boost the health culture within the Company and 
prompt the employees to value and pay attention to their health.
■ Employee Assistance Programs (EAPs) 
The Company has been working on EAPs in collaboration with the Hsinchu City Lifeline 
Association to oﬀer employees unlimited initial consultations and 4 free expert consultations 
and provide them with a sound support system. They can consult about problems related to 
marriage, family, parent-child relationships, ﬁnancial management, and laws, and we will help 
them properly deal with the problems that aﬀect their physical and mental health.
■ Soothing Massage for Employees
The Company actively fulfilled corporate social responsibilities 
by working with the Enlightenment Association for the 
Disadvantaged in Keelung City to offer employees a soothing 
massage service. This service was not only widely welcomed by 
the employees, but also highlighted the Company’s attention 
to social responsibilities. In 2022, we held 89 massage sessions, 
participated by 1,674 employees.
■ Health Knowledge Promotion 
With the aim of improving employees’ health knowledge and self-management abilities, the 
Company shared health information with the employees from time to time via email and 
the Yang Ming Monthly, YM You & Me. In 2022, 11 columns about occupational safety were 
issued to provide the latest health knowledge and helpful management tips in order for the 
employees to better manage their health.
■ Onboard Telemedical Consultation Services
Yang Ming collaborated with Keelung Hospital of the Ministry of Health and Welfare in 
oﬀering seafarers telemedical consultation services. All medical needs at sea are treated as 
Level 1 needs in ER and require professional medical doctors to give advice or determine 
if seafarers are in need of emergency hospitalization based on the medical suppliers and 
medicines on the vessel. In 2022, 134 at-sea medical consultations were carried out, providing 
comprehensive medical support for seafarers.
■ Flu Vaccination at the Company in Collaboration with the Qidu District 
     Public Health Center
In support of the government’s vaccination policy, Yang Ming made a request to the Qidu 
District Public Health Center to send medical staﬀ to the Company to provide ﬂu vaccination 
for our employees so as to protect their own health, their families, and the overall health 
of the Company. Headed by the Chairman, hundreds of employees waited in line for the 
vaccination, demonstrating their high-level determination to protect themselves and the 
entire organization.
Statistics of Health Promotion Activities in 2022: 
●25 health lectures, with 2,818 participants
●8 EAPs communication campaigns and 1 seafarer EAPs communication campaign,  
    participated by 50 seafarers
●89 massage sessions, with 1,674 participants.
●11 columns about occupational safety published in the Yang Ming Monthly, YM

■Health Management Platform
The Company has established health risk classiﬁcation management criteria to identify employees 
at high health risk based on their health checkup results. Such employees are provided with the 
necessary care and advice, helping them improve their health progressively. To cope with the fact 
that the existing manual work mode and system functions could no longer meet actual needs due 
to the Company’s increasingly complex employee health management activities as a result of the 
increased number of employees, more regulatory requirements, higher health check-up frequencies, 
more detailed health check-ups as well as more diverse health promotion activities, the Company 
built an online health management platform in 2022 and planned to use this platform to help the 
Company achieve the following short-term/medium-term/long-term goals:
1. Combination with Existing Functions Related to Health Management and Promotion
Activities: Planning, reservation, activity reminder, implementation result, subsequent tracking and
reminder, activity history search, and indicator analysis and comparison functions are integrated into 
the same platform for easy daily management, reducing manual work time and improving operational 
eﬃciency.
2. Post-Health Checkup Health Management: Employees at a high level of health risk may
be identified based on the default health management classification criteria and prioritized for
health consultations and tracking as well as subsequent health management, replacing the manual 
determination process to increase operational eﬃciency and save work time.
3. Health Indicator Management: This enables quick generation of work reports and analysis
reports to make health management plans and review outcomes based on individuals or groups’ 
health trend changes, enhancing operational eﬃciency and saving work time.
4. Health Checkup Data Input Management: Health checkup data may be input in the speciﬁed 
format, reducing manual work time and boosting work eﬃciency.
5. Improvement of Health Management Services: The convenience of use by employees e.g.
making activity reservations, receiving notiﬁcations, viewing and searching personal health data, and 
implementing subsequent self-health management is increased, thereby building good personal
health habits.
■Implementation of the Four Hazard Prevention Plans as Required by Law
▶Prevention of Ergonomic Engineering Hazar
Office operations are mainly performed in the Company’s working environment, and some 
employees are stevedore or dockworker banksmen, signalers or workers. After the Occupational 
Safety & Health Oﬃce reviewed the Company’s workplaces and working environments in support 
of the Ministry of Labor’s “Ergonomic Prevention Measures,” it found that the Company’s 
employees have been subjected to potential hazards of musculoskeletal disorders and eyestrain 
arising from long-term computer use, and therefore, it has promoted diﬀerent health promotion 
activities on a continuous basis ever since, including:
Providing large monitors or dual monitors for the employees to increase eye comfort; 
purchasing ergonomic oﬃce desks and chairs, reducing discomfort after sitting for a long time.
Working with on-site service doctors to launch the “Ergonomics – Walking Around Service” 
where the Company’s employees in diﬀerent regions are provided with assistance in making 
individual adjustments and finding the sitting posture that best suits them as well as health 
education; inviting physical therapists from Taipei Veterans General Hospital and Cathay General 
Hospital to give health lectures at the Company, sharing tips to prevent “ergonomic hazards” 
and providing health care advice to encourage the employees’ self-care to get rid of stiﬀness in 
back muscles.
Collaborating with the Keelung City Government and Enlightenment Association for the 
Disadvantaged to oﬃcially engage 9 visually-impaired massagists in November 2022 to provide 
massage services. Through muscle relaxation massage (20 minutes per session), employees’ 
stress can be reduced, thereby boosting work eﬃciency.
Organizing a 15-minute “Office Aerobics” session in every afternoon, where employees may 
choose to do aerobics (stretching) or stroll/walk around the sports field to limber up and 
enhance their cardiopulmonary function.

▶ Maternal Health Protection
The Company engages professional medical staff to give workplace health guidance for 
workplace maternal protection and provide individual job suitability assessments and 
advice, sets up well-equipped breastfeeding rooms, and grants prenatal examination leave, 
paternity leave or unpaid parental leave as required by law. In 2022, 15 female employees 
and 2 male employees (within 1 year after their spouses’ childbirth) participated in the 
maternal protection plan where they completed 5 face-to-face interviews with the Company’s 
contracted doctors for hazard identiﬁcation, risk assessment and job suitability assessment 
and were provided with health education and information during pregnancy and postpartum 
periods. Other maternal care actions are as follows:
Work adjustment: If on-site service doctors determine that the work or work location of 
pregnant employees requires adjustments, the Human Resources Department will contact 
the employees concerned and adjust their work or work location.
Flextime system: It not only allows employees to avoid the trouble of commuting during 
rush hours, but also makes it convenient to take care of their families or pick up their 
children.
Preschool service center: Set up in 2022, the center is open for employees to send their 
children here, freeing them of work and life worries.
Breastfeeding-friendly spaces: Taking the headquarters in Cidu as an example, its 
breastfeeding room has been ranked first in Keelung City for 6 consecutive years. The 
breastfeeding room is equipped with an exclusive sink, a baby-bottle steam sterilizer, a 
breast milk fridge, and a baby bottle cleaning detergent. What’s more, in consideration 
of the fact that the low temperature duration during winter in Keelung is relatively longer, 
heating equipment and blankets are also provided, and exclusive hangers are available 
for female employees to hang their clothes, oﬀering them a heartwarming and stress-free 
breastfeeding environment.
▶ Prevention of Illegal Infringement
The Company has established the “Procedures for Sexual Harassment Prevention, Whistleblowing 
and Punishment” to protect the individuality/dignity and personal freedom of the Company’s 
workers, job seekers, and business counterparties, provide a working environment free of sexual 
harassment, and adopt proper preventive, corrective, and punishment measures against sexual 
harassment incidents. To prevent the occurrence of sexual harassment incidents, promotion 
posters have been pasted in the Company’s oﬃces and public premises to raise gender equality 
awareness throughout the Company. The Human Resources Department is responsible for 
communicating and delivering sexual harassment prevention knowledge and skills to ingrain the 
concept of gender equality in the Company. The seed staff for sexual harassment prevention 
communicates relevant prevention measures from time to time to internal departments, and the 
Marine Department is responsible for communicating the measures to seafarers.
In investigating a sexual harassment complaint involving onshore employees, the complaint 
should be submitted to the Sexual Harassment Complaint Handling Committee for arbitration. If 
the complaint of sexual harassment is substantiated after the arbitration, it should be presented 
to the Human Resources Committee to determine the punishment in accordance with the 
Reward and Punishment Procedures for the Company’s Onshore Employees. If a complaint of 
sexual harassment involving seafarers is substantiated after arbitration, it should be presented 
to the Seafarer Arbitration Committee to determine the punishment pursuant to the Reward 
and Punishment Procedures for Seafarers or the employee contract or the agreement with the 
seafarer agency. In 2022, there were no illegal infringement and sexual harassment 
incidents involving onshore employees and seafarers.
▶ Prevention of Diseases Caused by Abnormal Workload
According to the Ministry of Labor’s guidelines, the Company has formulated the “Plan for 
Prevention of Diseases Caused by Abnormal Workload” for the Company’s workplaces with over 
100 employees. To ensure more accurate control of employees’ cardiovascular health conditions, 
Yang Ming has collaborated with health checkup hospitals to calculate the employees’ incidence 
of cardiovascular diseases in 10 years based on their health checkup results. We schedule health 
consultations with doctors for employees at higher risk, where they need to complete a 10-year 
cardiovascular disease risk assessment form and are given proper advice. Subsequently, health 
promotion activities are organized, including health lectures, weight loss classes, health-related 
physical ﬁtness activities, and nutrition education lectures, allowing the employees to make their 
lives healthy and reduce their health risks.
Onshore Employees
Seafarers
1,407 people completed the online 
“gender equality and sexual harassment 
prevention” propaganda course in 2022, 
with a test pass rate of 91.13%.
●Before boarding, seafarers are provided with training courses, 
      including what EAPs are, what they cover, and how to utilize them.

     campaign (2 hours) held during the onshore large-scale officer 
       training on December 19, 2022 was participated by 50 employees.

6.1 Yang Ming’s Community Care Strategies
Yang Ming has been dedicated to promoting ocean cultures and education and supporting the development of local communities. With “enhancing social participation to give back to society” 
as one of our sustainable development strategies, we demonstrate our empathy while developing our business, work with government organizations, charities, academic organizations, and 
NGOs in support of humanitarian and charitable aid, value the education and development of young people and students, oﬀer education subsidies, expand the seafarer manpower pool, and 
donate important practical teaching equipment required for professional seafarer training to maritime schools. Furthermore, in line with the sports policies implemented by the government, 
the Company sponsors excellent athletes and those with potential. Yang Ming also actively facilitates community development to encourage the promotion of local cultures.Yang Ming “spreads” 
happiness to society, cares for more communities, and heads toward the future of sustainable development.
  
Humanitarian and charitable aid About NT$12 million
Sponsorship of sports events, promotion of local 
cultural activities About NT$5 million
Industry-academia collaboration and teaching 
equipment donation About NT$35 million
Yang Ming has provided support for international emergency relief organizations (for wars, refugees) 
and domestic social welfare organizations. The Company encouraged onboard and onshore employees 
to support the year-end donation campaign of Yang Ming’s welfare club to put kindness into action and 
collect and provide physical resources to organizations for the vulnerable in Taiwan. In 2022, a total of 779 
employees participated in the campaign and made donations to up to 19 charities.
In 2022, the Company sponsored the organization of the Citizens Sports Games and actively assisted 
the government in the location where the headquarters is located in promoting cultural activities e.g. by 
supporting the organization of the Keelung Fairy Tales Festival and Keelung City Expo in 2022. Diﬀerent 
ocean education and promotion activities were organized through the YM Oceanic Culture & Art Museum 
to give knowledge of the cultures of Keelung Port. The YM Oceanic Culture & Art Museum also put out calls 
for shipping- and ocean-themed picture book submissions to convey and give knowledge of the shipping 
industry and the idea of a sustainable ocean and donated picture books to the elementary schools and 
junior high schools in Keelung City for the promotion of ocean cultures/education and local cultures.
We encouraged young people and students to enter the ocean shipping sector by oﬀering scholarships to 
enrich our marine talent pool. Important teaching equipment required for professional seafarer training 
was donated to maritime schools at all levels to bridge the gap between education and employment and 
jointly develop maritime talent.

  Flea Market Event in 2022
Since 2010, Yang Ming has followed 
the tradition continued for years and 
organized an internal anniversary 
charitable flea market at the end 
of every year. Our employees have 
actively donated items for charity 
sales. In 2022, 1,785 items were 
received and traded at the market 
to make the best use of items that 
were still useable to realize the idea 
of environmental protection by 
cherishing what we have and fully 
putting environmental protection into 
practice. This year, we also invited 
the “Taoyuan City Merry House 
Social Welfare Foundation,” “Genesis 
Social Welfare Foundation,” “Gofe 
Sheltered Workshop,” “Victory 
Kitchen of Taipei City Victory Social 
Welfare Foundation,” “I can LOHAS 
Workshop of Taipei Autism Children 
Social Welfare Foundation” and other charities to the charitable ﬂea market in the 
hope of encouraging our employees to purchase the products of the charities for 
support through the event.
Thanks to the fervent support and purchases by the employees in the ﬂea market, 
there were 664 items sold, including the ship models sold at an online auction and 
the company gifts available for sale onsite. This year’s charitable proceeds totaling 
NT$209,518 along with the year-end charitable donations from our employees 
were donated to the organizations for the vulnerable in need through the Huashan 
Social Welfare Foundation in continuation of Yang Ming’s care for society so as to 
inject positive energy into more charities and jointly grow with the society.
Promotion of Ocean Cultures and 
Connection with Local Communities
Inaugurated in 1915, the building of the YM Oceanic Culture & 
Art Museum, subordinate to the Yang Ming Cultural Foundation, 
has carried the memories and seaport stories of carriers and 
seafarers during the long-term historical development of ocean 
transportation at Keelung Port. The YM Oceanic Culture & Art 
Museum was founded at the end of 2004. It has put years of 
development eﬀorts in local communities and actively invited local 
organizations’ engagement for connection and co-creation. It has 
been over a year since the Keelung 1915 YM Oceanic Culture & Art 
Museum was renovated and started anew in 2021. By launching 
experiential activities well designed for diﬀerent communities and 
combined with shipping knowledge in a friendly and funny way, 
people are deeply connected with the land of Keelung. We hope 
that this can build local consensus, create a sense of identity, 
boost the cultural competence of people in the communities, 
give knowledge of shipping and life on the sea, offer the chance 
to experience seaport cultures, and attract attention to ocean 
sustainability issues, preserving historical memories for Keelung. 
The foundation will continue to convey Yang Ming’s ESG values 
and ocean cultures to the public in diverse and creative ways and 
implement social welfare activities.

  Ballast Water Animation and 365-degree 
Panoramic View of Container Ships
In 2022, the YM Oceanic Culture & Art Museum teamed up with the Industrial Technology Research Institute 
(ITRI) to integrate a model of the latest 2,800 TEU container ship, “YM Continent,” in the museum with the 
“interactive transparent display augmented reality technology” supported by the Ministry of Economic 
Aﬀairs and developed and designed by the ITRI and integrate the marine environment sustainability issues 
that Yang Ming values into the design to transform static displays into dynamic interactions. Such digital 
technology delivers an unprecedented visiting experience to visitors and successfully simpliﬁes abstruse ESG 
issues. The container ship model displayed in the museum has been 3D modelled and a smart touch display 
is installed by the physical ship model. People can feel free to touch the virtual ship model in the display by 
zooming in or out to view the container ship from all angles. 
With the description in the 3 animations and 3 games, a 
clear understanding of the basic structure and equipment 
of merchant ships can be given. Through dynamic data 
combined with marine ecology images, the 3D 365-degree 
panoramic animations introduce how ballast water keeps 
large cargo vessels balanced without overturning on the 
rough sea and what environmental protection measures 
should be adopted to maintain marine ecology.
  Love & Life, KEELUNG
To celebrate the opening of the National Square in front 
of the Keelung 1915 YM Oceanic Culture & Art Museum, 
the museum that is also located by the port organized the 
Love & Life Bazaar, musical performances, and multiple 
themed tours supported by local organizations, introducing 
the culture and life at Keelung Port to participants from 
various perspectives. During the two-day event, the museum 
extended its opening hours and people could visit the 
museum for free. The event attracted a total of over 5,201 
participants.
  Searching the Seaport for 26 hours!
The ocean is tied closely to the history of this city. Every 
line inﬂuences the movement of people in Keelung Port. 
As tides come and go, the hustle and bustle of the city is 
ongoing. The shipping stories occurring in Keelung are 
also the stories of people in this city. The YM Oceanic 
Culture & Art Museum worked together with Clubon to 
release the real escape game, “Searching the Seaport for 
26 hours!”. The game combined the exhibitions in the 
museum and the spots outside the museum to guide 
tourists through the downtown attractions in the west 
coast of Keelung Port, including the Harbor Building, 
commission store block, and Chenghuang Temple, 
enabling them to complete tasks while getting introduced 
to Keelung and the shipping industry! With a movie-like 
storyline loved by young people, the game engaged young 
players in exploring, from the museum to Keelung Port, to 
complete team tasks, successfully leading them into the 
museum in a game-playing manner.

Appendix
80% of the world’s daily necessities and cargo trading relies on 
marine transport. After huge container vessels reach the end 
of their lives, the steel hull plates removed therefrom can be 
melted and recycled. Ship parts, old instruments and equipment, 
and obsolete materials are still of value. Shui-Yan Yang, a 
designer good at hardware creation, finds multiple possibilities 
and imaginations for using waste container ship parts in life, 
successfully integrating shipping into life and delivering the 
sustainability value of waste material recycling. Important 
container ship parts are cleverly hidden in every piece of artwork. In this exhibition, visitors could learn about 
special parts on container ships from recycled works and know their features and applications. From the sketches 
of the designer, the visitors could slowly come up with various imaginations about objects on the sea and get to 
know more about and observe them with diﬀerent approaches. The visitors could therefore start to pay attention 
to environmental protection issues from an industrial perspective and discover the recyclability of waste items. 
  Goods Re-Thinking -  
Obsolete Ship Part Recycling Project Exhibition
  Environmental Classroom
The Yang Ming Cultural Foundation collaborated with First 
Bank in organizing the “Carbon Reduction Leader Summer 
Camp” to jointly promote environmental sustainability 
issues through a cross-industry alliance. An ESG trend 
course was organized specifically for students for the first 
time. The course was combined with various activities, 
including games, board games, exhibition visits, and port 
cruises. As the environment is changing, sustainable 
development has become a common language for all. 
The camp provided environmental education from an 
industrial perspective to deliver synergy benefits and give 
the public an understanding of how to promote a zero 
carbon environment and life at all levels, from individuals 
to industries! From the top 2 industries to how to find a 
balance between economy and environmental sustainability, 
the camp also designed courses exclusive for the children 
who want to experience and learn about various jobs, are 
newborns to international trading, and care about the future 
of the Earth.
  
Seafarer Activities for Kids -  
A Day in the Life of a Seafarer
The “A Day in the Life of a Seafarer” activities designed exclusively 
for parents and children are integrated with games designed 
based on Yang Ming’s ESG elements. Through interactive games 
involving driving a container trailer and stacker, lifting containers, 
and mooring a ship with ropes, they can enjoy parent-child 
interactions, know Keelung Port by “playing”, and understand 
what it is like to work onshore at the port dock. These games also 
help promote the features of Keelung and convey Yang Ming’s 
determination to facilitate ocean sustainability. The children who 
complete these games receive a certiﬁcate of honor and a limited edition. Yang Ming souvenir to give them a 
sense of honor. The activities are thus popular among parents and children. A total of 547 families, totaling 1,094 
people, participated in the activities.

About 8 million tons of garbage ﬂow into the sea every year. Humans’ lack of knowledge about ocean conservation will cause unprecedented disasters for the Earth and 
ocean. Yang Ming replies on the ocean for operation and is well aware of the impact of ocean pollution on the environment, society and economy. We hope to convey the 
importance of ocean conservation through child education. The Yang Ming Cultural Foundation worked together with the Bureau of Environmental Protection, Keelung 
City, to promote the ideas of ocean sustainability and environmental protection. A call for illustrations combined with “telescope,” “clock,” and “vessel” elements was held 
to publish a picture book related to ocean protection issues. Well-known picture book authors were also invited to come up with the story. A publishing house was then 
engaged to publish the picture book. In October 2022, which was the month of ocean conservation, the foundation invited Sky Nien, a well-known children's picture book 
author, and suyu, the ﬁrst-prize author, was invited to read the new picture book, Listen, the Ocean is Singing! to help children follow the steps of the main girl character in 
the book to ﬁnd ways to stop ocean pollution, engaging the readers in taking action to protect the ocean. In 2022, the published picture books were sent to 7 elementary 
schools in Keelung City for the promotion of ocean friendliness-themed wordless picture books, ingraining the ideas of ocean sustainability and environmental protection in 
children.

Ocean Cleanup in Collaboration with Azure Alliance to Contribute to Biodiversity Preservation
The Ellen MacArthur Foundation, a foreign authoritative research foundation, warned in its report that there are currently 1.5 trillion 
tons of garbage in the ocean and about 8 million tons of garbage ﬂow into the ocean every year around the world, which could reach 
a height equivalent to over 200 Taipei 101s if piled up. If no action is taken, such an enormous amount of ocean plastic garbage will 
double by 2030; if no change is made, there will be more garbage than ﬁsh in the ocean by 2050. The ocean is not only the origin 
of marine life, but also carries the past, present, and future of Taiwan. The ocean is the “foundation of Taiwan,” and import/export 
shipping trading is one of the key pillars of Taiwan’s economic growth. While oﬀering high-quality transportation services, Yang Ming 
bears the responsibility for implementing environmental protection and engaging in ocean protection and sustainability. In response 
to the UN’s SDG 14 – Life below Water, the Company has dedicated itself to engagement in marine environment conservation and 
cleaning activities. There are currently 220 ﬁshing ports around Taiwan. However, due to a severe lack of cleaning equipment and 
failure in proper management, the garbage accumulated in the harbor may ﬂow into the ocean when the wind direction changes. 
In 2022, the Company teamed up with the Azure Alliance to implement a marine environment cleanup project. With the Azure 
Alliance’s “Ocean Trash Collector – Marine Vacuum Cleaner” creates a key line of defense that effectively prevents the flow of 
garbage from the land into the ocean, removes the ﬂoating ocean trash in the harbor, and introduces systematic solutions so as to 
bring back cleanness to the ocean. Each Marine Vacuum Cleaner can remove about 200 kilograms of ocean garbage from the ocean 
in one day and prevent about 52 metric tons of garbage from entering the ocean annually. Through smart technology, the goal of 
taking concrete actions to reduce ocean garbage was achieved. The garbage salvaged from the ocean was sorted, and some plastic 
objects were recycled and turned into practical desks and chairs, which are provided to Bitou Elementary School, forming an ocean 
waste recycling chain and giving plastic garbage that causes ocean pollution a second life. The promotion of corporate sustainability 
actions relies on the engagement of all employees. The Company also invited the staggered participation of all employees in 
education courses and programs where the Azure Alliance’s professional lecturers delivered environmental education and training 
to the participating employees and guided them through the onsite operation of the Marine Vacuum Cleaner and beach cleanups, allowing the employees to understand the 
marine environment and technology applications. Actual participation in the onsite activities helped foster the vocation of every employee for environmental sustainability actions 
and engage them in jointly creating a more sustainable and bluer future for the coastal environments in Taiwan.
In 2022, a total of 21 
education courses along 
with beach cleanups 
were organized

Sports Promotion to Light Up Hope
Yang Ming takes seriously the health of employees. We have encouraged 
them to build good exercise habits outside of work to maintain their 
physical and mental health and provided them with health checkups and 
club allowances. By organizing various health lectures and encouraging 
the employees to be more engaged in physical ﬁtness activities, Yang Ming 
has become an “iSports enterprise” certiﬁed by the Sports Administration, 
Ministry of Education. To create social co-prosperity and deliver care to the 
community, the Company has planned the cultivation of young and excellent 
professional athletes with potential in Taiwan through long-term fixed-
amount sponsorships since 2021. The Company hopes that the investment 
of corporate resources can facilitate the professional training and career 
development of players and enable more new sports stars to concentrate 
on training in a worry-free environment in order to cope with more diﬀerent 
challenges and strive for better results in competitions.

Sustainability Report
 
Independent assurance statement  
 
 
Scope and approach 
Yang Ming Marine Transport Corporation (‘Yang Ming’ or ‘the Company’) commissioned DNV Business Assurance 
Taiwan (“DNV ”) to undertake independent assurance of the 2022 ESG Report (the “Report”) for the year ended 31 
December 2022. 
We performed our work using DNV’s assurance methodology VeriSustainTM1, which is based on our professional 
experience, international assurance best practice including International Standard on Assurance Engagements 3000 
(ISAE 3000) and the Global Reporting Initiative (GRI) Sustainability Reporting Standards 2021.  
The Report also incorporated the relevant sustainability reporting guidelines, such as Sustainable Development Best 
Practice Principles for TWSE/TPEx Listed Companies, Marine Transportation SASB Standards, and TCFD. 
We understand that the reported financial data and information are based on data from Yang Ming Annual Report and 
Accounts, which are subject to a separate independent audit process. The review of financial data taken from the 
Annual Report and Accounts is not within the scope of our work. 
We planned and performed our work to obtain the evidence we considered necessary to provide a basis for our 
assurance opinion. We are providing the evaluation of reporting principles and selected performance information with a 
Moderate level of assurance, according to the DNV VeriSustainTM. 
Responsibilities of the Directors of Yang Ming Marine Transport 
Corporation and of the assurance providers 
The Directors of YANG MING have sole responsibility for the preparation of the Report.  In performing our assurance 
work, our responsibility is to the management of YANG MING; however, our statement represents our independent 
opinion and is intended to inform all of YANG MING stakeholders.  DNV was not involved in the preparation of any 
statements or data included in the Report except for this Assurance Statement.  
DNV provides a range of other services to Yang Ming, none of which constitute a conflict of interest with this assurance 
work. This is the 7th year that we have provided assurance. 
DNV’s assurance engagements are based on the assumption that the data and information provided by the client to us 
as part of our review have been provided in good faith.  DNV expressly disclaims any liability or co-responsibility for any 
decision a person or an entity may make based on this Assurance Statement. 
 
Basis of our opinion 
 
A multi-disciplinary team of sustainability and assurance specialists performed work at headquarters and site level.  We 
undertook the following activities:  
 
• 
Review of the current corporate responsibility issues that could affect YANG MING and are of interest to stakeholders; 
• 
Review of YANG MING’s approach to stakeholder engagement and recent outputs; 
• 
Review of information provided to us by YANG MING on its reporting and management processes relating to the Principles; 
• 
Interviews with selected Directors and senior managers responsible for management of corporate responsibility issues and review 
of selected evidence to support issues discussed; 
• 
Review process and systems for preparing site level corporate responsibility data and implementation of corporate responsibility 
strategy; 
• 
Review of supporting evidence for key claims and 2022 data in the report. Our checking processes were prioritised according to 
materiality and we based our prioritisation on the materiality of issues at a consolidated corporate level; 
• 
Review of the processes for gathering and consolidating the specified performance data and, for a sample, checking the data 
consolidation. Where financial data had been checked by another third party, and, where data of ships’ Green House Gases 
Emission has been verified by DNV, we tested transposition from these sources to the report. 
• 
An independent assessment of Yang Ming reporting against the Global Reporting Initiative (GRI) Sustainability Reporting 
Standards (2021). 
• 
The verification was conducted based only on the Chinese version Report. 
 
 
1 The VeriSustain protocol is available on dnv.com

This Verification Opinion is based on the information made available to us and the engagement conditions detailed above. Hence, DNV cannot guarantee the 
accuracy or correctness of the information. DNV cannot be held liable by any party relying or acting upon this Verification Opinion. 
立恩威國際驗證股份有限公司, 新北市板橋區文化路二段293 號29 樓, TEL : +886-2-82537800, website:www.dnv.com/tw

Issued date:

This is to verify initiate reporting of Greenhouse Gas Inventory Management Report (2022) of 
YANG MING MARINE TRANSPORT 
CORPORATION 
Scope of Verification 
DNV Business Assurance (DNV) has been commissioned by YANG MING MARINE TRANSPORT 
CORPORATION (hereafter  ‘the Organization’) to perform a verification of the greenhouse gas 
statements of Greenhouse Gas Inventory Management Report (2022) (hereafter the “Inventory 
Report”) in Taiwan, ROC with respect to the sites listed in Appendix A. 
The Reporting Boundary for the verification including direct GHG emissions and removals, indirect GHG 
emissions from imported energy, indirect GHG emissions from transportation, indirect GHG emissions 
from products used by the Organization and indirect GHG emissions associated with the use of products 
from the Organization. The further descriptions for the Reporting Boundary listed in Appendix B and C.  
Verification Criteria and GHG Programme 
The verification was performed on the basis of ISO 14064-1:2018 as well as criteria given to provide for 
consistent GHG emission identification, calculation, monitoring and reporting. 
The verification was conducted in accordance with ISO 14066:2011, ISO 14065:2013, ISO14064-
3:2019 
Verification Statement 
It is DNV’s opinion that the Inventory Report (2022), which was published on April 2023 (Ver. I), is free 
from material discrepancies in accordance with the verification criteria identified as stated above. The 
opinion is decided based on the following approaches, 
− 
For the Direct (Category 1) and Indirect GHG emissions from imported energy (Category 2), the 
reliability of the information within the Inventory Report (2022) were verified with reasonable 
level of assurance.  
− 
For the other indirect GHG emissions, the involved information was verified and tested using 
agreed-upon procedures, AUP, defined in Inventory Report.  
Also, the GHG information as stated in Appendix B and C has been verified during the process. 
 
Chun-Nan Lin
